<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0; text-align: left">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0; text-align: center">Schedule 5&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Tax
covenant</P>

<P STYLE="font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0; text-align: center">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: small-caps bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 0"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 0.5in"><FONT STYLE="font-variant: normal; text-transform: uppercase">1.</FONT></TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify">Interpretation</TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify; text-indent: -0.5in">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 0"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 0.5in">1.1</TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify">The definitions and rules of interpretation in this paragraph apply in this Tax Covenant.</TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify"><B>&nbsp;</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify"><B>Accounts Relief:</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 0 77.95pt; text-align: justify; text-indent: -28.35pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 49.6pt"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 28.35pt">(a)</TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify">any Relief (including the right to a repayment of Tax) that has been shown as an asset in the Completion
Statements; and</TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 0 77.95pt; text-align: justify; text-indent: -28.35pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 49.6pt"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 28.35pt">(b)</TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify">any Relief that has been taken into account in computing (and so reducing or eliminating) any provision
for deferred Tax in the Completion Statements.</TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify"><B>&nbsp;</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify"><B>Buyer's Relief:</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 0 77.95pt; text-align: justify; text-indent: -28.35pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 49.6pt"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 28.35pt">(a)</TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify">any Accounts Relief;</TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 0 77.95pt; text-align: justify; text-indent: -28.35pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 49.6pt"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 28.35pt">(b)</TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify">any Relief which arises in connection with any Event occurring after Completion; and</TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 0 77.95pt; text-align: justify; text-indent: -28.35pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 49.6pt"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 28.35pt">(c)</TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify">any Relief, whenever arising, of the Buyer or any member of the Buyer's Tax Group other than the
Companies and the Subsidiaries.</TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify"><B>&nbsp;</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify"><B>Buyer's Tax Group:</B> the Buyer
and any other company or companies which are from time to time treated as members of the same group as, or otherwise connected
or associated in any way with, the Buyer for any Tax purpose.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify"><B>&nbsp;</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify"><B>Dispute:</B> any dispute, appeal,
negotiations or other proceedings in connection with a Tax Claim.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify"><B>&nbsp;</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify"><B>Event:</B> includes (without limitation),
the expiry of a period of time, the Companies or any Subsidiary becoming or ceasing to be associated with any other person for
any Tax purpose or ceasing to be or becoming resident in any country for any Tax purpose, the death or the winding up or dissolution
of any person, the earning, receipt or accrual for any Tax purpose of any income, profit or gains, the incurring of any loss or
expenditure, and any transaction (including the execution and completion of all provisions of this agreement), event, act or omission
whatsoever, and any reference to an Event occurring on or before a particular date shall include Events which, for Tax purposes,
are deemed to have, or are treated or regarded as having, occurred on or before that date.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify"><B>&nbsp;</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify"><B>Liability for Taxation:</B> means:</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 0 77.95pt; text-align: justify; text-indent: -28.35pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 49.6pt"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 28.35pt">(a)</TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify">any liability of the Companies or any Subsidiary to make a payment of or in respect of Tax, whether
or not the same is primarily payable by the Companies or the relevant Subsidiary and whether or not the Companies or the relevant
Subsidiary has or may have any right of reimbursement against any other person or persons, in which case the amount of the Liability
for Taxation shall be the amount of the actual payment;</TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 0 77.95pt; text-align: justify; text-indent: -28.35pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 49.6pt"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 28.35pt">(b)</TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify">the Loss of any Accounts Relief in which case the amount of the Liability for Taxation will be
the amount of Tax which would (on the basis of Tax rates current at the date of such Loss) have been saved but for such Loss, assuming
for this purpose that the Companies or the relevant Subsidiary had sufficient profits or was otherwise in a position to use the
Relief or where the Relief is the right to repayment of Tax, the amount of the repayment;</TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0; text-align: left">&nbsp;</P>


<!-- Field: Page; Sequence: 50; Value: 1 -->
    <DIV STYLE="margin-top: 12pt; margin-bottom: 6pt; border-bottom: Black 1pt solid"><TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" STYLE="width: 100%; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif"><TR><TD STYLE="text-align: center; width: 100%"><!-- Field: Sequence; Type: Arabic; Name: PageNo -->49<!-- Field: /Sequence --></TD></TR></TABLE></DIV>
    <DIV STYLE="page-break-before: always; margin-top: 6pt; margin-bottom: 12pt"><TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" STYLE="width: 100%; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif"><TR><TD STYLE="text-align: center; width: 100%">&nbsp;</TD></TR></TABLE></DIV>
    <!-- Field: /Page -->

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0; text-align: left">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 49.6pt"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 28.35pt">(c)</TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify">the use or setting off of any Buyer's Relief in circumstances where, but for such set off or use,
the Companies or the relevant Subsidiary would have had a liability to make a payment of or in respect of Tax for which the Buyer
would have been able to make a claim against the Sellers under this Tax Covenant, in which case, the amount of the Liability for
Taxation shall be the amount of Tax for which the Sellers would have been liable but for such set off or utilisation.</TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify"><B>&nbsp;</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify"><B>Loss:</B> any reduction, modification,
loss, counteraction, nullification, utilisation, disallowance or clawback for whatever reason.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify"><B>&nbsp;</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify"><B>Overprovision:</B> the amount
by which any provision for tax (other than deferred tax) in the Completion Statements is overstated, except where such overstatement
arises as a result of:</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 0 77.95pt; text-align: justify; text-indent: -28.35pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 49.6pt"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 28.35pt">(a)</TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify">a change in law;</TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 0 77.95pt; text-align: justify; text-indent: -28.35pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 49.6pt"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 28.35pt">(b)</TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify">a change in the accounting bases on which the Companies or any Subsidiary values its assets; or</TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 0 77.95pt; text-align: justify; text-indent: -28.35pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 49.6pt"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 28.35pt">(c)</TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify">a voluntary act or omission of the Buyer</TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify">which, in each case, occurs after
Completion.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify"><B>&nbsp;</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify"><B>Relief:</B> includes any loss,
relief, allowance, credit, exemption or set off in respect of Tax or any deduction in computing income, profits or gains for the
purposes of Tax and any right to a repayment of Tax.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify"><B>&nbsp;</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify"><B>Saving:</B> the reduction or elimination
of any liability of the Companies or a Subsidiary to make an actual payment of corporation tax in respect of which the Sellers
would not have been liable under paragraph 2, by the use of any Relief arising wholly as a result of a Liability for Taxation in
respect of which the Sellers have made a payment under paragraph 2 of this Tax Covenant.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify"><B>&nbsp;</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify"><B>Tax or Taxation:</B> all forms
of taxation and statutory, governmental, state, federal, provincial, local, government or municipal charges, duties, imposts, contributions,
levies, withholdings or liabilities wherever chargeable and whether of the UK or any other jurisdiction (including, for the avoidance
of doubt, National Insurance contributions in the UK and corresponding obligations elsewhere) and any penalty, fine, surcharge,
interest, charges or costs relating thereto (including interest and penalties arising from the failure of the Company or any Subsidiary
to make adequate instalment payments under the Corporation Tax (Instalments Payments) Regulations 1998 (<I>SI 1998/3175</I>) in
any period ending on or before Completion).</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify"><B>&nbsp;</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify"><B>Tax Claim:</B> any assessment,
notice, demand, letter or other document issued or action taken by or on behalf of any Taxation Authority, self-assessment or other
occurrence from which it appears that the Buyer, the Companies or a Subsidiary is or may be subject to a Liability for Taxation
or other liability in respect of which the Sellers are or may be liable under this Tax Covenant.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify"><B>&nbsp;</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify"><B>Taxation Authority:</B> any government,
state or municipality or any local, state, federal or other fiscal, revenue, customs or excise authority, body or official competent
to impose, administer, levy, assess or collect Tax in the UK or elsewhere.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0; text-align: left">&nbsp;</P>


<!-- Field: Page; Sequence: 51; Value: 1 -->
    <DIV STYLE="margin-top: 12pt; margin-bottom: 6pt; border-bottom: Black 1pt solid"><TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" STYLE="width: 100%; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif"><TR><TD STYLE="text-align: center; width: 100%"><!-- Field: Sequence; Type: Arabic; Name: PageNo -->50<!-- Field: /Sequence --></TD></TR></TABLE></DIV>
    <DIV STYLE="page-break-before: always; margin-top: 6pt; margin-bottom: 12pt"><TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" STYLE="width: 100%; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif"><TR><TD STYLE="text-align: center; width: 100%">&nbsp;</TD></TR></TABLE></DIV>
    <!-- Field: /Page -->

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0; text-align: left">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify"><B>Taxation Statute:</B> any directive,
statute, enactment, law or regulation wheresoever enacted or issued, coming into force or entered into providing for or imposing
any Tax and shall include orders, regulations, instruments, bye-laws or other subordinate legislation made under the relevant statute
or statutory provision and any directive, statute, enactment, law, order, regulation or provision which amends, extends, consolidates
or replaces the same or which has been amended, extended, consolidated or replaced by the same.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 0"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 0.5in">1.2</TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify">References to gross receipts, income, profits or gains earned, accrued or received shall include
any gross receipts, income, profits or gains deemed under the relevant Taxation Statute to have been or treated or regarded as
earned, accrued or received.</TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify; text-indent: -0.5in">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 0"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 0.5in">1.3</TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify">References to a repayment of Tax shall include any repayment supplement or interest in respect
of it.</TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify; text-indent: -0.5in">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 0"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 0.5in">1.4</TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify">Any reference to something occurring in the ordinary course of business shall not include:</TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 0 77.95pt; text-align: justify; text-indent: -28.35pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 49.6pt"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 28.35pt">(a)</TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify">anything that involves, or leads directly or indirectly to, any liability of the Companies or the
relevant Subsidiary to Tax (other than VAT, PAYE or NIC arising in the ordinary course of business) that is, or but for an election
would have been, the primary liability of, or properly attributable to, or due from another person (other than a member of the
Buyer's Tax Group);</TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 0 77.95pt; text-align: justify; text-indent: -28.35pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 49.6pt"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 28.35pt">(b)</TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify">anything that relates to or involves the acquisition or disposal of an asset or the supply of services
(including the lending of money, or the hiring or licensing of tangible or intangible property) in a transaction to the extent
to which it is not entered into on arm's length terms;</TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 0 77.95pt; text-align: justify; text-indent: -28.35pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 49.6pt"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 28.35pt">(c)</TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify">anything that relates to or involves the making of a distribution for Tax purposes, the creation,
cancellation or re-organisation of share or loan capital, the creation, cancellation or repayment of any connected-party debt or
the Companies or any Subsidiary becoming or ceasing to be or being treated as ceasing to be a member of a group of companies or
becoming or ceasing to be associated or connected with any other company for any Tax purposes;</TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 0 77.95pt; text-align: justify; text-indent: -28.35pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 49.6pt"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 28.35pt">(d)</TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify">anything which relates to any scheme, transaction or arrangement designed partly or wholly or containing
steps or stages partly or wholly for the purpose of avoiding or reducing or deferring a Liability for Taxation;</TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 0 77.95pt; text-align: justify; text-indent: -28.35pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 49.6pt"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 28.35pt">(e)</TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify">anything that gives rise to a Liability for Taxation on deemed (as opposed to actual) profits or
to the extent that it gives rise to a Liability for Taxation on an amount of profits greater than the difference between the sale
proceeds of an asset and the amount attributable to that asset in the Accounts or, in the case of an asset acquired since the Accounts
Date, the cost of that asset; or</TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 0 77.95pt; text-align: justify; text-indent: -28.35pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 49.6pt"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 28.35pt">(f)</TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify">anything that involves, or leads directly or indirectly to, a change of residence of the Companies
or any Subsidiary for Tax purposes.</TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 0 77.95pt; text-align: justify; text-indent: -28.35pt">&nbsp;</P>

same meaning in this Tax Covenant and any provisions in this agreement concerning matters of construction or interpretation also
apply in this Tax Covenant.</TD></TR></TABLE>

<TD STYLE="width: 0"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 0.5in"><FONT STYLE="font-variant: normal; text-transform: uppercase">3.</FONT></TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify">Payment date and interest</TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify; text-indent: -0.5in">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 0"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 0.5in">3.1</TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify">Payment by the Sellers in respect of any liability under this Schedule must be made in cleared
and immediately available funds on the following days:</TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 0 77.95pt; text-align: justify; text-indent: -28.35pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 49.6pt"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 28.35pt">(a)</TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify">in the case of a Liability for Taxation that involves an actual payment of or in respect of Tax,
the later of seven Business Days before the due date for payment and seven Business Days after the date on which the Buyer serves
notice on the Sellers requesting payment;</TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 0 77.95pt; text-align: justify; text-indent: -28.35pt">&nbsp;</P>

the date on which the Buyer serves notice on the Sellers requesting payment and (ii) the date the repayment of Tax would have arisen
assuming HMRC had made the repayment as soon as it became due;</TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 0 77.95pt; text-align: justify; text-indent: -28.35pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">

of (i) seven Business Days following the date on which the Buyer serves notice on the Sellers requesting payment and (ii) the last
date on which the Tax is or would have been required to be paid to the relevant Taxation Authority in respect of</TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 0 113.4pt; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0in">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 0 113.4pt; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0in">the period in
which the Loss of the Relief gives rise to an actual liability to pay tax;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 0 77.95pt; text-align: justify; text-indent: -28.35pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 49.6pt"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 28.35pt">(d)</TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify">in a case that falls within paragraph 1.1(c) of the definition of Liability for Taxation, the date
on which the Tax saved by the Companies or the relevant Subsidiary is or would have been required to be paid to the relevant Taxation
Authority; or</TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 0 77.95pt; text-align: justify; text-indent: -28.35pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 49.6pt"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 28.35pt">(e)</TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify">in the case of a liability arising under paragraph 2.1(g), seven Business Days following the date
on which the Buyer serves notice on the Sellers requesting payment.</TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 0 77.95pt; text-align: justify; text-indent: -28.35pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 0"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 0.5in">3.2</TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify">If any sums required to be paid by the Sellers under this Tax Covenant are not paid on the date
specified in paragraph 3.1, then, except to the extent that the Sellers' liability under paragraph 2 compensates the Buyer for
the late payment by virtue of it extending to interest and penalties, such sums shall bear interest (which shall accrue from day
to day after as well as before any judgment for the same) at the rate of 2% per annum over the base rate from time to time of Barclays
Bank Plc or (in the absence thereof) at such similar rate as the Buyer shall select from the day following the Due Date up to and
including the day of actual payment of such sums, such interest to be compounded quarterly.</TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify; text-indent: -0.5in">&nbsp;</P>

<TD STYLE="width: 0"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 0.5in"><FONT STYLE="font-variant: normal; text-transform: uppercase">8.</FONT></TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify">Corporation tax returns</TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify; text-indent: -0.5in">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 0"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 0.5in">8.1</TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify">Subject to this paragraph 8, the Buyer will have exclusive conduct of all Taxation affairs of the
Companies and the Subsidiaries after Completion.</TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify; text-indent: -0.5in">&nbsp;</P>

<TD STYLE="width: 0"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 0.5in">8.2</TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify">The Sellers or their duly authorised agent shall at the Sellers' cost and expense prepare the corporation
tax returns and computations of the Companies and the Subsidiaries for all accounting periods ended on or before the Accounts Date,
to the extent that the same have not been prepared before Completion, and submit them to the Buyer.</TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify; text-indent: -0.5in">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 0"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 0.5in">8.3</TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify">The Buyer shall procure that the returns and computations referred to in paragraph 8.2 shall be
authorised, signed and submitted to the relevant Taxation Authority without amendment or with such amendments as the Buyer reasonably
considers to be necessary and shall give the Sellers or their agent all such assistance as may reasonably be required (at the Sellers'
cost and expense) to agree those returns and computations with the relevant Taxation Authority provided that the Buyer shall not
be obliged to take any such action as is mentioned in this paragraph 8.3 in relation to any return that is not full, true and accurate
in all material respects.</TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify; text-indent: -0.5in">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 0"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 0.5in">8.4</TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify">The Sellers or their duly authorised agent shall at the Sellers' cost and expense prepare all documentation
and shall have conduct of all matters (including correspondence) relating to the corporation tax returns and computations of the
Companies and the Subsidiaries for all accounting periods ended on or prior to the Accounts Date provided that the Sellers shall
not without the prior written consent of the Buyer (not to be unreasonably withheld or delayed) transmit any communication (written
or otherwise) to the relevant Taxation Authority or agree any matter with the relevant Taxation Authority.</TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify; text-indent: -0.5in">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 0"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 0.5in">8.5</TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify">The Buyer shall procure that the Companies and the Subsidiaries, at the Sellers' cost and expense,
afford such access to their books, accounts and records as is necessary and reasonable to enable the Sellers or their duly authorised
agent to prepare the corporation tax returns and computations of the Companies and the Subsidiaries for all accounting periods
ended on or before the Accounts Date and conduct matters relating to them in accordance with this paragraph 8.</TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify; text-indent: -0.5in">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 0"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 0.5in">8.6</TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify">The Sellers shall take all reasonable steps to ensure that the corporation tax returns and computations
of the Companies and the Subsidiaries for all accounting periods ended on or before the Accounts Date are prepared and agreed with
the relevant Taxation Authority as soon as possible.</TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify; text-indent: -0.5in">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" STYLE="width: 100%; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top; text-align: justify">
<TD STYLE="width: 0"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 0.5in; text-align: left">8.7</TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify">In respect of the accounting period commencing prior to
Completion and ending after Completion (&ldquo;<B>Straddle Period</B>&rdquo;) the Buyer shall procure that the corporation tax
returns and computations shall be prepared in a manner consistent with past practices and without a change of any accounting method
(except to the extent necessary to comply with applicable law or the rules of the SEC or the Trading Market).</TD>
</TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify; text-indent: -0.5in">&nbsp;</P>

and computations relating to the Straddle Period no later than ten Business Days before the date on which such returns and computations

<TD STYLE="width: 0"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 0.5in">8.9</TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify">For the avoidance of doubt:</TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 49.6pt"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 28.35pt">(a)</TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify">where any matter relating to Tax gives rise to a Tax Claim, the provisions of paragraph 9 shall
take precedence over the provisions of this paragraph 8; and</TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 0 77.95pt; text-align: justify; text-indent: -28.35pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">

under this Tax Covenant in respect of any Liability for Taxation.</TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 0 77.95pt; text-align: justify; text-indent: -28.35pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: small-caps bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 0"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 0.5in"><FONT STYLE="font-variant: normal; text-transform: uppercase">9.</FONT></TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify">Conduct of tax claims</TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify; text-indent: -0.5in">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 0"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 0.5in">9.1</TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify">Subject to paragraph 9.2, if the Buyer or the Companies or a Subsidiary becomes aware of a Tax
Claim, the Buyer shall give or procure that notice in writing is given to the Sellers or to the Sellers' duly appointed agent as
soon as is reasonably practicable, provided that the Buyer shall not be required to give or procure the giving of such notice if
there is any allegation that any of the Sellers (or any of the Targets before Completion) has been involved in fraudulent conduct
which constitutes a criminal offence under French or UK legislation in respect of the subject matter of the Tax Claim. If a notice
of a tax audit is received by the Buyer, the Companies or a Subsidiary the Buyer shall ensure that a copy of such notice is given
to the Sellers as soon as is reasonably practicable. The giving of such notice as referred to in this paragraph 9.1 shall not be
a condition precedent to the Sellers&rsquo; liability under this Tax Covenant.</TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify; text-indent: -0.5in">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 0"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 0.5in">9.2</TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify">If the Sellers become aware of a tax audit or Tax Claim, they shall notify the Buyer in writing
as soon as reasonably practicable, and in any case no later than ten Business Days after the Sellers, the Companies or a Subsidiary
are made aware of such tax audit or Tax Claim. Upon receipt of such notice, the Buyer shall be deemed to have given the Sellers
notice of the tax audit or Tax Claim in accordance with the provisions of paragraph 9.1.</TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify; text-indent: -0.5in">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 0"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 0.5in">9.3</TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify">Subject to paragraph 9.4, provided the Sellers indemnify the Buyer against all liabilities, costs,
damages or expenses which may be incurred by the Buyer and the Targets thereby including any additional Liability for Taxation,
the Buyer shall take and shall procure that the Companies or the relevant Subsidiary shall take such action as the Sellers may
reasonably request by notice in writing given to the Buyer to avoid, dispute, defend, resist, appeal, request an internal HM Revenue
&amp; Customs review or compromise any Tax Claim. Any payment made under the indemnity in this paragraph 9.3 by MOBIFLUX shall
not be deemed to be a reduction in Purchase Price, but rather shall be treated as a pure indemnity, which is payable to the Buyer
or alternatively, should the Buyer in its sole discretion so elect (notwithstanding clause 9 and schedule 2.1 of Schedule 5 of
this agreement) to Farncombe UK or Farncombe ES.</TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0; text-align: left">&nbsp;</P>

against any assessment to Tax if the Buyer, having given the Sellers written notice of such assessment, does not receive written
instructions from the Sellers within twenty Business Days to do so.</TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify; text-indent: -0.5in">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 0 77.95pt; text-align: justify; text-indent: -28.35pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 49.6pt"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 28.35pt">(a)</TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify">the Sellers do not request the Buyer to take any action under paragraph 9.3 or fail to indemnify
the Buyer, or the Companies to the Buyer's reasonable satisfaction within a period of time (commencing with the date of the notice
given to the Sellers) that is reasonable, having regard to the nature of the Tax Claim and the existence of any time limit in relation
to avoiding, disputing, defending, resisting, appealing, requesting a review or compromising such Tax Claim, and which period shall
not in any event exceed a period of twenty Business Days;</TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 0 77.95pt; text-align: justify; text-indent: -28.35pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 49.6pt"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 28.35pt">(b)</TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify">any of the Sellers (or the Companies or any Subsidiary before Completion) has been involved in
a case involving fraudulent conduct or deliberate default in respect of the Liability for Taxation which is the subject matter
of the Dispute; or</TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 0 77.95pt; text-align: justify; text-indent: -28.35pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">

(or, for appeals lodged before 1 April 2009, a determination by the Tax Chamber of the First-tier Tribunal or Higher Tribunal),
unless the Sellers have obtained the opinion of Tax counsel of at least five years' standing that there is a reasonable prospect
that the appeal will succeed,</TD></TR></TABLE>

relevant Subsidiary shall have the conduct of the Dispute absolutely (without prejudice to its rights under this Tax Covenant)
and shall be free to pay or settle the Tax Claim on such terms as the Buyer, or the Companies or that Subsidiary may in its absolute
discretion consider fit.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

to any of the Sellers for non-compliance with any of the foregoing provisions of this paragraph 9 if the Buyer, or the Company
has bona fide acted in accordance with the instructions of any one or more of the Sellers.</TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify; text-indent: -0.5in">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: small-caps bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 0"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 0.5in"><FONT STYLE="font-variant: normal; text-transform: uppercase">10.</FONT></TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify">Grossing up</TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify; text-indent: -0.5in">&nbsp;</P>

<TD STYLE="width: 0"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 0.5in">10.1</TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify">All sums payable by the Sellers to the Buyer and/or by the Buyer to the Sellers under this Tax
Covenant shall be paid free and clear of all deductions or withholdings whatsoever unless the deduction or withholding is required
by law. If any deductions or withholdings are required by law to be made from any of the sums payable under this Tax Covenant,
the Sellers shall pay to the Buyer such sum as will, after the deduction or withholding has been made, leave the Buyer with the
same amount as it would have been entitled to receive in the absence of any such requirement to make a deduction or withholding.</TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0; text-align: center">Schedule 7&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Completion Statements</P>

<P STYLE="font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0; text-align: center; text-indent: 0in">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0; text-align: center">Part&nbsp;1: General</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify; text-indent: -0.5in"><FONT STYLE="font-weight: normal">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 0"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 0.5in"><FONT STYLE="font-weight: normal">1.</FONT></TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify">Contents</TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify; text-indent: -0.5in"><FONT STYLE="font-weight: normal">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 0"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 0.5in"></TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-weight: normal">The Completion Statements shall comprise (i) the balance sheets
of each of the Companies and the Subsidiaries and a statement of the May Net Working Capital as at close of business on 31 May
2015; and (ii) the balance sheets of each of the Companies and the Subsidiaries and a statement of the Completion Net Working Capital
as at close of business on the Completion Date, in the form and including the items set out in Part&nbsp;3 of this Schedule.</FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify; text-indent: -0.5in"><FONT STYLE="font-weight: normal">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 0"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 0.5in"><FONT STYLE="font-weight: normal">2.</FONT></TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify">Bases of preparation</TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify">The Completion Statements shall be
prepared:</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 0 70.9pt; text-align: justify; text-indent: -35.45pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 35.45pt"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 35.45pt">2.1</TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify">in accordance with the specific accounting treatments set out in Part 4 of this Schedule; and subject
thereto;</TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 0 70.9pt; text-align: justify; text-indent: -35.45pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 35.45pt"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 35.45pt">2.2</TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify">adopting the same accounting policies, principles, estimation techniques, measurement bases, practices
and procedures used in the preparation of the Accounts as there applied; and subject thereto;</TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 0 70.9pt; text-align: justify; text-indent: -35.45pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 35.45pt"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 35.45pt">2.3</TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify">in accordance with the Accounting Standards in force and mandatory in the United Kingdom (for Farncombe
UK and Farncombe ES) or in France (for Farncombe France) at the Completion Date.</TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify; text-indent: -0.5in"><FONT STYLE="font-weight: normal">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 0"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 0.5in"><FONT STYLE="font-weight: normal">3.</FONT></TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify">Submission of Draft Completion Statements</TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 0 70.9pt; text-align: justify; text-indent: -35.45pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 35.45pt"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 35.45pt">3.1</TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify">The Sellers shall procure the preparation and submission to the Buyer of a draft of the Completion
Statements (&ldquo;<B>Draft Completion Statements</B>&rdquo;) within 30&nbsp;Business Days of Completion.</TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 0 70.9pt; text-align: justify; text-indent: -35.45pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 35.45pt"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 35.45pt">3.2</TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify">Within 15&nbsp;Business Days of receipt of the Draft Completion Statements (&ldquo;<B>Response
Period</B>&rdquo;), the Buyer shall give notice to the Sellers (&ldquo;<B>Response Notice</B>&rdquo;) stating whether or not the
Buyer agrees with the Draft Completion Statements.</TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 0 70.9pt; text-align: justify; text-indent: -35.45pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 35.45pt"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 35.45pt">3.3</TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify">If the Buyer disagrees with the Draft Completion Statements, the Response Notice shall also state:</TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 0 113.4pt; text-align: justify; text-indent: -42.5pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 70.9pt"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 42.5pt">3.3.1</TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify">the item or items in dispute;</TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 0 113.4pt; text-align: justify; text-indent: -42.5pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 70.9pt"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 42.5pt">3.3.2</TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify">the reasons for such dispute; and</TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 0 106.9pt; text-align: justify; text-indent: -0.5in">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 70.9pt"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 36pt">3.3.3</TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify">(to the extent then reasonably practicable) details of its proposed adjustments to the Draft Completion
Statements.</TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify; text-indent: -0.5in"><FONT STYLE="font-weight: normal">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 0"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 0.5in"><FONT STYLE="font-weight: normal">4.</FONT></TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify">No Response Notice</TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify">If the Buyer does not give the Response
Notice within the Response Period, then the Buyer shall be deemed to have agreed the Draft Completion Statements, and such statements
shall constitute the Completion Statements.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0; text-align: left">&nbsp;</P>

<TD STYLE="width: 0"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 0.5in"><FONT STYLE="font-weight: normal">5.</FONT></TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify">Positive Response Notice</TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify">If the Response Notice is given within

the Completion Statements.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify; text-indent: -0.5in"><FONT STYLE="font-weight: normal">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 0"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 0.5in"><FONT STYLE="font-weight: normal">6.</FONT></TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify">Negative Response Notice</TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify">If the Response Notice is given within
the Response Period and states that the Buyer disagrees with the Draft Completion Statements, then:</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 0 70.9pt; text-align: justify; text-indent: -35.45pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 35.45pt"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 35.45pt">6.1</TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify">the Buyer and the Sellers shall enter into negotiations and endeavour to agree the items disputed
by the Buyer in the Response Notice in good faith;</TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 0 70.9pt; text-align: justify; text-indent: -35.45pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 35.45pt"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 35.45pt">6.2</TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify">only those items detailed as disputed in the Response Notice that remain in dispute after the negotiation
between the Buyer and Sellers pursuant to paragraph&nbsp;6.1 above (&ldquo;<B>Disputed Items</B>&rdquo;) shall be treated as being
in dispute, and the Buyer and Sellers shall be deemed to have agreed all other items in the Draft Completion Statements;</TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 0 70.9pt; text-align: justify; text-indent: -35.45pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 35.45pt"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 35.45pt">6.3</TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify">if, within 10 Business Days of receipt of the Response Notice, all the Disputed Items are resolved
by agreement between them, the Buyer and the Sellers shall promptly sign a joint statement which:</TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 0 106.9pt; text-align: justify; text-indent: -0.5in">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 70.9pt"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 36pt">6.3.1</TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify">appends a copy of the Draft Completion Statements, adjusted to reflect all the Disputed Items as
so agreed; and</TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 0 106.9pt; text-align: justify; text-indent: -0.5in">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 70.9pt"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 36pt">6.3.2</TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify">confirms that such accounts constitute the Completion Statements;</TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 0 70.9pt; text-align: justify; text-indent: -35.45pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 35.45pt"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 35.45pt">6.4</TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify">if, within 10&nbsp;Business Days of receipt of the Response Notice, the Buyer and the Sellers have
not agreed the Completion Statements in accordance with paragraph&nbsp;6.3:</TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 0 106.9pt; text-align: justify; text-indent: -0.5in">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 70.9pt"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 36pt">6.4.1</TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify">where relevant, the Buyer and the Sellers shall promptly sign a joint statement which:</TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 0 2in; text-align: justify; text-indent: -37.65pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 106.35pt"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 37.65pt">6.4.1.1</TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify">sets out the Disputed Items (if any) that have been agreed between them; and</TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 0 2in; text-align: justify; text-indent: -37.65pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 106.35pt"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 37.65pt">6.4.1.2</TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify">appends a copy of the Draft Completion Statements, adjusted to reflect any Disputed Item as so
agreed; and</TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 0 106.9pt; text-align: justify; text-indent: -0.5in">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 70.9pt"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 36pt">6.4.2</TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify">the remaining Disputed Items shall be referred for determination by an Expert in accordance with
the provisions of Part&nbsp;2 of this Schedule upon the written request of either the Buyer or the Sellers&rsquo; Representative;
and</TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 0 70.9pt; text-align: justify; text-indent: -35.45pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 35.45pt"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 35.45pt">6.5</TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify">if the Buyer and the Sellers do not agree the Completion Statements in accordance with paragraph&nbsp;6.3,
then the Draft Completion Statements adjusted to reflect:</TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 0 106.9pt; text-align: justify; text-indent: -0.5in">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 70.9pt"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 36pt">6.5.1</TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify">the Disputed Items (if any) that are agreed between the Sellers&rsquo; Representative and the Buyer
in writing (whether in accordance with paragraph&nbsp;6.4.1 or subsequently); and</TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 0 106.9pt; text-align: justify; text-indent: -0.5in">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 70.9pt"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 36pt">6.5.2</TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify">the Expert&rsquo;s determination made pursuant to Part&nbsp;2 of this Schedule,</TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 0 70.9pt; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 0 70.9pt; text-align: justify">shall constitute the Completion
Statements.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0; text-align: left">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0; text-align: left"></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 0 70.9pt; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 0"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 0.5in">7.</TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify"><B>Records and access</B></TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify">From Completion until the agreement,
deemed agreement or determination of the Completion Statements, each of the Buyer and the Sellers shall:</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 0 70.9pt; text-align: justify; text-indent: -35.45pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 35.45pt"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 35.45pt">7.1</TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify">retain any relevant records, documents and information within its possession or under its or their
control (which, for the avoidance of doubt, shall not include auditors&rsquo; working papers) relating to the assets, liabilities
and other matters which are the subject of the Completion Statements (<B>&ldquo;Completion Statements Information&rdquo;</B>);
and</TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 0 70.9pt; text-align: justify; text-indent: -35.45pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 35.45pt"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 35.45pt">7.2</TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify">provide to the others and their representatives such access to:</TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 0 106.9pt; text-align: justify; text-indent: -0.5in">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 70.9pt"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 36pt">7.2.1</TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify">any assets of the Companies and the Subsidiaries within its possession or under its control; and</TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 0 106.9pt; text-align: justify; text-indent: -0.5in">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 70.9pt"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 36pt">7.2.2</TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify">such of its accounting records and its personnel to obtain all relevant facts and information within
their knowledge (except any document and/or information that was prepared by another party or its advisers with a view to assessing
the merits of any argument on any Disputed Item or that is otherwise legally privileged),</TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 0 70.9pt; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 0 70.9pt; text-align: justify">as is reasonably required by the
others to prepare, review, agree or otherwise determine the Completion Statements (as appropriate).</P>

<P STYLE="font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0; text-align: center; text-indent: 0in">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0; text-align: center; text-indent: 0in">Part&nbsp;2: Expert determination</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify; text-indent: -0.5in"><FONT STYLE="font-weight: normal">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 0"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 0.5in"><FONT STYLE="font-weight: normal">1.</FONT></TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify">Appointment of Expert</TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify">Each of the Buyer and the Sellers
agrees to:</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 0 70.9pt; text-align: justify; text-indent: -35.45pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 35.45pt"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 35.45pt">1.1</TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify">use its reasonable endeavours to appoint an Expert expeditiously following a written request to
do so from the other and to agree the terms of engagement for the Expert within 10&nbsp;Business Days of the Expert&rsquo;s selection
or nomination; and</TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 0 70.9pt; text-align: justify; text-indent: -35.45pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 35.45pt"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 35.45pt">1.2</TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify">not unreasonably (having regard to the provisions of this Part&nbsp;2) refuse its agreement to
any terms of engagement proposed by the Expert (which may include a limitation on his liability at a level consistent with market
practice at the relevant time) or the other party.</TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify; text-indent: -0.5in">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 0"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 0.5in">2.</TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify"><B>Procedure</B></TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 0 70.9pt; text-align: justify; text-indent: -35.45pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 35.45pt"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 35.45pt">2.1</TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify">The Buyer and the Sellers shall each supply the other with a copy of any written submission provided
by it or on its behalf to the Expert pursuant to this Part&nbsp;2 at the same time as it is provided to the Expert.</TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 0 70.9pt; text-align: justify; text-indent: -35.45pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 35.45pt"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 35.45pt">2.2</TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify">Within 5&nbsp;Business Days of the appointment of the Expert, the Sellers&rsquo; Representative
shall provide the Expert with the following:</TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 0 106.9pt; text-align: justify; text-indent: -0.5in">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 70.9pt"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 36pt">2.2.1</TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify">a copy of the Draft Completion Statements (adjusted to reflect the Disputed Items (if any) then
agreed between the Buyer and the Sellers&rsquo; Representative in writing) (&ldquo;<B>Adjusted Draft Completion Statements</B>&rdquo;);
and</TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 0 106.9pt; text-align: justify; text-indent: -0.5in">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 70.9pt"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 36pt">2.2.2</TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify">a written statement of the Disputed Items referred to the Expert as referred to in paragraph&nbsp;6.4.2
above.</TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0; text-align: left">&nbsp;</P>

    <DIV STYLE="margin-top: 12pt; margin-bottom: 6pt; border-bottom: Black 1pt solid"><TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" STYLE="width: 100%; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif"><TR><TD STYLE="text-align: center; width: 100%"><!-- Field: Sequence; Type: Arabic; Name: PageNo -->64<!-- Field: /Sequence --></TD></TR></TABLE></DIV>
    <DIV STYLE="page-break-before: always; margin-top: 6pt; margin-bottom: 12pt"><TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" STYLE="width: 100%; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif"><TR><TD STYLE="text-align: center; width: 100%">&nbsp;</TD></TR></TABLE></DIV>
    <!-- Field: /Page -->

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0; text-align: left"></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 0 106.9pt; text-align: justify; text-indent: -0.5in">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 35.45pt"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 35.45pt">2.3</TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify">Each of the Buyer and the Sellers shall provide (or, to the extent it is reasonably able, procure
that others provide) the Expert with such documents, information and assistance (including the right to inspect the Completion
Statements Information) as the Expert reasonably requires for the purpose of making his determination.</TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 0 70.9pt; text-align: justify; text-indent: -35.45pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 35.45pt"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 35.45pt">2.4</TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify">All matters in relation to any determination under this Part&nbsp;2 shall be kept confidential
by the parties and the Expert.</TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 0 70.9pt; text-align: justify; text-indent: -35.45pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 35.45pt"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 35.45pt">2.5</TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify">To the extent not provided for in or inconsistent with this Part&nbsp;2, the Expert shall determine
the procedure to be followed in making his determination and shall be entitled to obtain such independent legal or other professional
advice as he may reasonably require in making his determination.</TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify; text-indent: -0.5in">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 0"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 0.5in">3.</TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify"><B>Role of Expert</B></TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 0 70.9pt; text-align: justify; text-indent: -35.45pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 35.45pt"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 35.45pt">3.1</TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify">The Expert shall:</TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 0 106.9pt; text-align: justify; text-indent: -0.5in">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 70.9pt"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 36pt">3.1.1</TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify">determine on the basis of all information, documents and materials before him what adjustments
(if any) are in his opinion necessary to the amounts shown by the Adjusted Draft Completion Statements in respect of each of the
Disputed Items referred to him in order to comply with the provisions of this agreement; and</TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 0 106.9pt; text-align: justify; text-indent: -0.5in">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 70.9pt"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 36pt">3.1.2</TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify">notify the parties of his determination in writing (without reasons) as soon as reasonably practicable
and in any event within 30 Business Days of his appointment.</TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0; text-align: center; text-indent: 0in">Part&nbsp;4: Specific
accounting treatments</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0; text-align: left">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0; text-align: center"><B>Omitted</B></P>

    <DIV STYLE="margin-top: 12pt; margin-bottom: 6pt; border-bottom: Black 1pt solid"><TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" STYLE="width: 100%; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif"><TR><TD STYLE="text-align: center; width: 100%"><!-- Field: Sequence; Type: Arabic; Name: PageNo -->67<!-- Field: /Sequence --></TD></TR></TABLE></DIV>
    <DIV STYLE="page-break-before: always; margin-top: 6pt; margin-bottom: 12pt"><TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" STYLE="width: 100%; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif"><TR><TD STYLE="text-align: center; width: 100%">&nbsp;</TD></TR></TABLE></DIV>
